[2;36m                    [0m         # Evaluation Report                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Summary                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         An AddressSanitizer report has identified a heap-buffer-overflow in the FreeRDP     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         codebase. The overflow occurs when Stream_Read attempts an [1;36m8[0m-byte write immediately [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         past the end of a [1;36m992[0m-byte heap allocation. This error surfaces during the          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         processing of a client “conference create” request in the GCC [1m([0mGlobal Channel       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         Connection[1m)[0m code, triggered by the fuzzing harness in TestFuzzCoreServer.           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Description                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Issue Type                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           The error is a heap-buffer-overflow: an [1;36m8[0m-byte write occurs at the byte           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         immediately following a [1;36m992[0m-byte heap allocation.                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Faulting Location                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           The overflow is detected in Stream_Read [1m([0mwinpr/stream.h:[1;36m703[0m[1m)[0m. Stream_Read is      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         called from gcc_read_client_network_data, which is part of the GCC message parsing  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         logic in libfreerdp/core/gcc.c.                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Allocation Site                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           The buffer was allocated by a call to calloc in mcs_new                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1m([0mlibfreerdp/core/mcs.[1;92mc:1446[0m[1m)[0m, which sets up MCS [1m([0mMultipoint Communication Service[1m)[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         structures. The allocated region spans [1;36m992[0m bytes, and the overflow write lands      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         exactly at offset [1;36m992[0m.                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Call Stack Highlights                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [1;36m1[0m. Stream_Read [1m([0mwinpr/stream.h:[1;36m703[0m[1m)[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [1;36m2[0m. gcc_read_client_network_data [1m([0mlibfreerdp/core/gcc.[1;92mc:1875[0m[1m)[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [1;36m3[0m. gcc_read_client_data_blocks [1m([0mlibfreerdp/core/gcc.[1;92mc:617[0m[1m)[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [1;36m4[0m. gcc_read_conference_create_request [1m([0mlibfreerdp/core/gcc.[1;92mc:414[0m[1m)[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [1;36m5[0m. mcs_recv_connect_initial [1m([0mlibfreerdp/core/mcs.[1;92mc:700[0m[1m)[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [1;36m6[0m. freerdp_is_valid_mcs_create_request [1m([0mlibfreerdp/core/freerdp.[1;92mc:1441[0m[1m)[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [1;36m7[0m. test_server harness [1m([0mTestFuzzCoreServer.c[1m)[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [1;36m8[0m. LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput → FuzzerDriver → main                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Observations and Findings                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           • The write occurs exactly [1;36m0[0m bytes past the end of the allocated region,          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         indicating missing or incorrect bounds checks.                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           • The vulnerability is exposed under the client “conference create” request code  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         path.                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           • The fuzzing harness [1m([0mTestFuzzCoreServer[1m)[0m invokes the vulnerable path but is not [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         the root cause; it merely drives the input into the parsing logic.                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           • Deduplication tokens in the report confirm the overflow is tied to Stream_Read  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         → gcc_read_client_network_data → gcc_read_client_data_blocks.                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Areas for Investigation                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           To understand the full context of this issue, the following components should be  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         examined:                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           • Stream_Read implementation and its handling of buffer lengths and remaining     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         bytes.                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           • gcc_read_client_network_data and gcc_read_client_data_blocks for how they       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         calculate and verify the size of incoming data.                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           • gcc_read_conference_create_request for any length fields or offsets used when   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         reading the conference create structure.                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           • mcs_new and mcs_recv_connect_initial in mcs.c, where the heap buffer is         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         allocated and the initial connection structures are populated.                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           • freerdp_is_valid_mcs_create_request in freerdp.c, which orchestrates MCS        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         request validation.                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           • Any upstream size or boundary validations in the protocol parsing code that     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         feed into Stream_Read.                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         No speculation on underlying causes or remediation strategies is included in this   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         report.                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAn AddressSanitizer heap-buffer-overflow was reported in FreeRDP’s Stream_Read [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfunction [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwinpr/include/winpr/stream.h[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m when processing client network data in the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mGCC path. The overflow involved an [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m-byte write immediately past a [0m[1;36m992[0m[39m-byte heap [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallocation made in `mcs_new`. A patch was applied to change the Stream_Read [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39massertion from checking `Stream_GetRemainingCapacity` to [0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`Stream_GetRemainingLength`. Despite that change, re-running the fuzzer produced [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe same heap-buffer-overflow at the same location in Stream_Read.[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mInitial Issue  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- AddressSanitizer flagged a write of [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m bytes at the very end of a [0m[1;36m992[0m[39m-byte region [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallocated by `calloc` in `mcs_new`.  [0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The overflow occurred in Stream_Read [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwinpr/include/winpr/stream.h:[0m[1;36m703[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m when [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minvoked via `gcc_read_client_network_data` → `gcc_read_client_data_blocks` → [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`gcc_read_conference_create_request` → `mcs_recv_connect_initial` → [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`freerdp_is_valid_mcs_create_request` → fuzz test harness.  [0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The report included a full backtrace of the write and the corresponding [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallocation stack trace.[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mImportant Observations  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The buffer was allocated with exactly [0m[1;36m992[0m[39m bytes, and the overflow write was at [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moffset [0m[1;36m992[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m0[0m[39m-based[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, i.e. just past the end.  [0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Stream_Read does a `[0m[1;35mmemcpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39m_b, _s->pointer, _n[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` followed by `[0m[1;35mStream_Seek[0m[1;39m([0m[39m_s, [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m_n[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.  [0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The assertion before the memcpy originally tested the remaining capacity of the [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstream.[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mPatch Attempt  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- In winpr/include/winpr/stream.h, the static inline definition of Stream_Read was [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmodified:  [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  * Old line:  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    `[0m[1;35mWINPR_ASSERT[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mStream_GetRemainingCapacity[0m[1;39m([0m[39m_s[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m >= _n[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`  [0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  * New line:  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    `[0m[1;35mWINPR_ASSERT[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mStream_GetRemainingLength[0m[1;39m([0m[39m_s[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m >= _n[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`  [0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- This ensures the check uses the remaining *length* [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbytes left to read[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m rather [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthan remaining *capacity*.  [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No other changes were made to the memcpy or seek logic.[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- AddressSanitizer still reports a heap-buffer-overflow in Stream_Read at the same [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msite [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m703[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The overflow occurs under the same test conditions and call stack, indicating the[0m [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
